# Koine Greek Lexicon

**Complete Dictionary of New Testament Greek**

Total Entries: 5523

---

## G1

**Greek:** Α

**Transliteration:** *A*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  the first letter of the alphabet; figuratively, only (from its use as a numeral) the first: 

**KJV Equivalents:** --Alpha

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin;

---

## G2

**Greek:** Ἀαρών

**Transliteration:** *Aarṓn*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Aaron, the brother of Moses

**KJV Equivalents:** Aaron

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H0175);

---

## G3

**Greek:** Ἀβαδδών

**Transliteration:** *Abaddṓn*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a destroying angel

**KJV Equivalents:** Abaddon

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H011);

---

## G4

**Greek:** ἀβαρής

**Transliteration:** *abarḗs*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  weightless, i.e. (figuratively) not burdensome

**KJV Equivalents:** from being burdensome

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and G922 (βάρος);

---

## G5

**Greek:** Ἀββᾶ

**Transliteration:** *Abbâ*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  father as a vocative

**KJV Equivalents:** Abba

**Etymology:** of Chaldee origin (H02);

---

## G6

**Greek:** Ἄβελ

**Transliteration:** *Ábel*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Abel, the son of Adam

**KJV Equivalents:** Abel

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H01893);

---

## G7

**Greek:** Ἀβιά

**Transliteration:** *Abiá*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Abijah, the name of two Israelites

**KJV Equivalents:** Abia

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H029);

---

## G8

**Greek:** Ἀβιαθάρ

**Transliteration:** *Abiathár*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Abiathar, an Israelite

**KJV Equivalents:** Abiathar

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H054);

---

## G9

**Greek:** Ἀβιληνή

**Transliteration:** *Abilēnḗ*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Abilene, a region of Syria

**KJV Equivalents:** Abilene

**Etymology:** of foreign origin (compare H058);

---

## G10

**Greek:** Ἀβιούδ

**Transliteration:** *Abioúd*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Abihud, an Israelite

**KJV Equivalents:** Abiud

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H031);

---

## G11

**Greek:** Ἀβραάμ

**Transliteration:** *Abraám*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Abraham, the Hebrew patriarch

**KJV Equivalents:** Abraham

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H085);

---

## G12

**Greek:** ἄβυσσος

**Transliteration:** *ábyssos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  depthless, i.e. (specially) (infernal) \

**KJV Equivalents:** deep, (bottomless) pit

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and a variation of G1037 (βυθός);

---

## G13

**Greek:** Ἄγαβος

**Transliteration:** *Ágabos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  Agabus, an Israelite

**KJV Equivalents:** Agabus

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (compare H02285);

---

## G14

**Greek:** ἀγαθοεργέω

**Transliteration:** *agathoergéō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to work good

**KJV Equivalents:** do good

**Etymology:** from G18 (ἀγαθός) and G2041 (ἔργον);

---

## G15

**Greek:** ἀγαθοποιέω

**Transliteration:** *agathopoiéō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to be a well-doer (as a favor or a duty)

**KJV Equivalents:** (when) do good (well)

**Etymology:** from G17 (ἀγαθοποιός);

---

## G16

**Greek:** ἀγαθοποιΐα

**Transliteration:** *agathopoiḯa*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  well-doing, i.e. virtue

**KJV Equivalents:** well-doing

**Etymology:** from G17 (ἀγαθοποιός);

---

## G17

**Greek:** ἀγαθοποιός

**Transliteration:** *agathopoiós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a well-doer, i.e. virtuous

**KJV Equivalents:** them that do well

**Etymology:** from G18 (ἀγαθός) and G4160 (ποιέω);

---

## G18

**Greek:** ἀγαθός

**Transliteration:** *agathós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  \

**KJV Equivalents:** benefit, good(-s, things), well

**Etymology:** a primary word;

---

## G19

**Greek:** ἀγαθωσύνη

**Transliteration:** *agathōsýnē*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  goodness, i.e. virtue or beneficence

**KJV Equivalents:** goodness

**Etymology:** from G18 (ἀγαθός);

---

## G20

**Greek:** ἀγαλλίασις

**Transliteration:** *agallíasis*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  exultation; specially, welcome

**KJV Equivalents:** gladness, (exceeding) joy

**Etymology:** from G21 (ἀγαλλιάω);

---

## G21

**Greek:** ἀγαλλιάω

**Transliteration:** *agalliáō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  properly, to jump for joy, i.e. exult

**KJV Equivalents:** be (exceeding) glad, with exceeding joy, rejoice (greatly)

**Etymology:** from agan (much) and G242 (ἅλλομαι);

---

## G22

**Greek:** ἄγαμος

**Transliteration:** *ágamos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  unmarried

**KJV Equivalents:** unmarried

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and G1062 (γάμος);

---

## G23

**Greek:** ἀγανακτέω

**Transliteration:** *aganaktéō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  akin to the base of G43 (ἀγκάλη)); to be greatly afflicted, i.e. (figuratively) indignant

**KJV Equivalents:** be much (sore) displeased, have (be moved with, with) indignation

**Etymology:** from (much) and (grief;

---

## G24

**Greek:** ἀγανάκτησις

**Transliteration:** *aganáktēsis*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  indignation

**KJV Equivalents:** indignation

**Etymology:** from G23 (ἀγανακτέω);

---

## G25

**Greek:** ἀγαπάω

**Transliteration:** *agapáō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to love (in a social or moral sense)

**KJV Equivalents:** (be-)love(-ed)

**Etymology:** perhaps from (much) (or compare G5689);

---

## G26

**Greek:** ἀγάπη

**Transliteration:** *agápē*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  love, i.e. affection or benevolence; specially (plural) a love-feast

**KJV Equivalents:** (feast of) charity(-ably), dear, love

**Etymology:** from G25 (ἀγαπάω);

---

## G27

**Greek:** ἀγαπητός

**Transliteration:** *agapētós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  beloved

**KJV Equivalents:** (dearly, well) beloved, dear

**Etymology:** from G25 (ἀγαπάω);

---

## G28

**Greek:** Ἄγαρ

**Transliteration:** *Ágar*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Hagar, the concubine of Abraham

**KJV Equivalents:** Hagar

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H01904);

---

## G29

**Greek:** ἀγγαρεύω

**Transliteration:** *angareúō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  properly, to be a courier, i.e. (by implication) to press into public service

**KJV Equivalents:** compel (to go)

**Etymology:** of foreign origin (compare H0104);

---

## G30

**Greek:** ἀγγεῖον

**Transliteration:** *angeîon*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  compare the base of G43 (ἀγκάλη)); a receptacle

**KJV Equivalents:** vessel

**Etymology:** from (a pail, perhaps as bent;

---

## G31

**Greek:** ἀγγελία

**Transliteration:** *angelía*

**Part of Speech:** noun

**Definition:**  an announcement, i.e. (by implication) precept

**KJV Equivalents:** message

**Etymology:** from G32 (ἄγγελος);

---

## G32

**Greek:** ἄγγελος

**Transliteration:** *ángelos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  compare G34 (ἀγέλη)) (to bring tidings); a messenger; especially an \

**KJV Equivalents:** angel, messenger

**Etymology:** from (probably derived from G71 (ἄγω);

---

## G33

**Greek:** ἄγε

**Transliteration:** *áge*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  properly, lead, i.e. come on

**KJV Equivalents:** go to

**Etymology:** imperative of G71 (ἄγω);

---

## G34

**Greek:** ἀγέλη

**Transliteration:** *agélē*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a drove

**KJV Equivalents:** herd

**Etymology:** from G71 (ἄγω) (compare G32 (ἄγγελος));

---

## G35

**Greek:** ἀγενεαλόγητος

**Transliteration:** *agenealógētos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  unregistered as to birth

**KJV Equivalents:** without descent

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as negative particle) and G1075 (γενεαλογέω);

---

## G36

**Greek:** ἀγενής

**Transliteration:** *agenḗs*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  properly, without kin, i.e. (of unknown descent, and by implication) ignoble

**KJV Equivalents:** base things

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as negative particle) and G1085 (γένος);

---

## G37

**Greek:** ἁγιάζω

**Transliteration:** *hagiázō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to make holy, i.e. (ceremonially) purify or consecrate; (mentally) to venerate

**KJV Equivalents:** hallow, be holy, sanctify

**Etymology:** from G40 (ἅγιος);

---

## G38

**Greek:** ἁγιασμός

**Transliteration:** *hagiasmós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  properly, purification, i.e. (the state) purity; concretely (by Hebraism) a purifier

**KJV Equivalents:** holiness, sanctification

**Etymology:** from G37 (ἁγιάζω);

---

## G39

**Greek:** ἅγιον

**Transliteration:** *hágion*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  a sacred thing (i.e. spot)

**KJV Equivalents:** holiest (of all), holy place, sanctuary

**Etymology:** neuter of G40 (ἅγιος);

---

## G40

**Greek:** ἅγιος

**Transliteration:** *hágios*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  sacred (physically, pure, morally blameless or religious, ceremonially, consecrated)

**KJV Equivalents:** (most) holy (one, thing), saint

**Etymology:** from (an awful thing) (compare G53 (ἁγνός), G2282 (θάλπω));

---

## G41

**Greek:** ἁγιότης

**Transliteration:** *hagiótēs*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  sanctity (i.e. properly, the state)

**KJV Equivalents:** holiness

**Etymology:** from G40 (ἅγιος);

---

## G42

**Greek:** ἁγιωσύνη

**Transliteration:** *hagiōsýnē*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  sacredness (i.e. properly, the quality)

**KJV Equivalents:** holiness

**Etymology:** from G40 (ἅγιος);

---

## G43

**Greek:** ἀγκάλη

**Transliteration:** *ankálē*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  an arm (as curved)

**KJV Equivalents:** arm

**Etymology:** from (a bend, \

---

## G44

**Greek:** ἄγκιστρον

**Transliteration:** *ánkistron*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  a hook (as bent)

**KJV Equivalents:** hook

**Etymology:** from the same as G43 (ἀγκάλη);

---

## G45

**Greek:** ἄγκυρα

**Transliteration:** *ánkyra*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  an \

**KJV Equivalents:** anchor

**Etymology:** from the same as G43 (ἀγκάλη);

---

## G46

**Greek:** ἄγναφος

**Transliteration:** *ágnaphos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  properly, unfulled, i.e. (by implication) new (cloth)

**KJV Equivalents:** new

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and the same as G1102 (γναφεύς);

---

## G47

**Greek:** ἁγνεία

**Transliteration:** *hagneía*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  cleanliness (the quality), i.e. (specially) chastity

**KJV Equivalents:** purity

**Etymology:** from G53 (ἁγνός);

---

## G48

**Greek:** ἁγνίζω

**Transliteration:** *hagnízō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to make clean, i.e. (figuratively) sanctify (ceremonially or morally)

**KJV Equivalents:** purify (self)

**Etymology:** from G53 (ἁγνός);

---

## G49

**Greek:** ἁγνισμός

**Transliteration:** *hagnismós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a cleansing (the act), i.e. (ceremonially) lustration

**KJV Equivalents:** purification

**Etymology:** from G48 (ἁγνίζω);

---

## G50

**Greek:** ἀγνοέω

**Transliteration:** *agnoéō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  not to know (through lack of information or intelligence); by implication, to ignore (through disinclination)

**KJV Equivalents:** (be) ignorant(-ly), not know, not understand, unknown

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and G3539 (νοιέω);

---

## G51

**Greek:** ἀγνόημα

**Transliteration:** *agnóēma*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a thing ignored, i.e. shortcoming

**KJV Equivalents:** error

**Etymology:** from G50 (ἀγνοέω);

---

## G52

**Greek:** ἄγνοια

**Transliteration:** *ágnoia*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  ignorance (properly, the quality)

**KJV Equivalents:** ignorance

**Etymology:** from G50 (ἀγνοέω);

---

## G53

**Greek:** ἁγνός

**Transliteration:** *hagnós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  properly, clean, i.e. (figuratively) innocent, modest, perfect

**KJV Equivalents:** chaste, clean, pure

**Etymology:** from the same as G40 (ἅγιος);

---

## G54

**Greek:** ἁγνότης

**Transliteration:** *hagnótēs*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  cleanness (the state), i.e. (figuratively) blamelessness

**KJV Equivalents:** pureness

**Etymology:** from G53 (ἁγνός);

---

## G55

**Greek:** ἁγνῶς

**Transliteration:** *hagnōs*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  purely, i.e. honestly

**KJV Equivalents:** sincerely

**Etymology:** adverb from G53 (ἁγνός);

---

## G56

**Greek:** ἀγνωσία

**Transliteration:** *agnōsía*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  ignorance (properly, the state)

**KJV Equivalents:** ignorance, not the knowledge

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as negative particle) and G1108 (γνῶσις);

---

## G57

**Greek:** ἄγνωστος

**Transliteration:** *ágnōstos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  unknown

**KJV Equivalents:** unknown

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as negative particle) and G1110 (γνωστός);

---

## G58

**Greek:** ἀγορά

**Transliteration:** *agorá*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  probably akin to G1453 (ἐγείρω)); properly, the town-square (as a place of public resort); by implication, a market or thoroughfare

**KJV Equivalents:** market(-place), street

**Etymology:** from (to gather;

---

## G59

**Greek:** ἀγοράζω

**Transliteration:** *agorázō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  properly, to go to market, i.e. (by implication) to purchase; specially, to redeem

**KJV Equivalents:** buy, redeem

**Etymology:** from G58 (ἀγορά);

---

## G60

**Greek:** ἀγοραῖος

**Transliteration:** *agoraîos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  relating to the market-place, i.e. forensic (times); by implication, vulgar

**KJV Equivalents:** baser sort, low

**Etymology:** from G58 (ἀγορά);

---

## G61

**Greek:** ἄγρα

**Transliteration:** *ágra*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  (abstractly) a catching (of fish); also (concretely) a haul (of fish)

**KJV Equivalents:** draught

**Etymology:** from G71 (ἄγω);

---

## G62

**Greek:** ἀγράμματος

**Transliteration:** *agrámmatos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  unlettered, i.e. illiterate

**KJV Equivalents:** unlearned

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as negative particle) and G1121 (γράμμα);

---

## G63

**Greek:** ἀγραυλέω

**Transliteration:** *agrauléō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to camp out

**KJV Equivalents:** abide in the field

**Etymology:** from G68 (ἀγρός) and G832 (αὐλέω) (in the sense of G833 (αὐλή));

---

## G64

**Greek:** ἀγρεύω

**Transliteration:** *agreúō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to hunt, i.e. (figuratively) to entrap

**KJV Equivalents:** catch

**Etymology:** from G61 (ἄγρα);

---

## G65

**Greek:** ἀγριέλαιος

**Transliteration:** *agriélaios*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  an oleaster

**KJV Equivalents:** olive tree (which is) wild

**Etymology:** from G66 (ἄγριος) and G1636 (ἐλαία);

---

## G66

**Greek:** ἄγριος

**Transliteration:** *ágrios*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  wild (as pertaining to the country), literally (natural) or figuratively (fierce)

**KJV Equivalents:** wild, raging

**Etymology:** from G68 (ἀγρός);

---

## G67

**Greek:** Ἀγρίππας

**Transliteration:** *Agríppas*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  wild-horse tamer; Agrippas, one of the Herods

**KJV Equivalents:** Agrippa

**Etymology:** apparently from G66 (ἄγριος) and G2462 (ἵππος);

---

## G68

**Greek:** ἀγρός

**Transliteration:** *agrós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a field (as a drive for cattle); genitive case, the country; specially, a farm, i.e. hamlet

**KJV Equivalents:** country, farm, piece of ground, land

**Etymology:** from G71 (ἄγω);

---

## G69

**Greek:** ἀγρυπνέω

**Transliteration:** *agrypnéō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to be sleepless, i.e. keep awake

**KJV Equivalents:** watch

**Etymology:** ultimately from G1 (Α) (as negative particle) and G5258 (ὕπνος);

---

## G70

**Greek:** ἀγρυπνία

**Transliteration:** *agrypnía*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  sleeplessness, i.e. a keeping awake

**KJV Equivalents:** watch

**Etymology:** from G69 (ἀγρυπνέω);

---

## G71

**Greek:** ἄγω

**Transliteration:** *ágō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  properly, to lead; by implication, to bring, drive, (reflexively) go, (specially) pass (time), or (figuratively) induce

**KJV Equivalents:** be, bring (forth), carry, (let) go, keep, lead away, be open

**Etymology:** a primary verb;

---

## G72

**Greek:** ἀγωγή

**Transliteration:** *agōgḗ*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a bringing up, i.e. mode of living

**KJV Equivalents:** manner of life

**Etymology:** reduplicated from G71 (ἄγω);

---

## G73

**Greek:** ἀγών

**Transliteration:** *agṓn*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  properly, a place of assembly (as if led), i.e. (by implication) a contest (held there); figuratively, an effort or anxiety

**KJV Equivalents:** conflict, contention, fight, race

**Etymology:** from G71 (ἄγω);

---

## G74

**Greek:** ἀγωνία

**Transliteration:** *agōnía*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a struggle (properly, the state), i.e. (figuratively) anguish

**KJV Equivalents:** agony

**Etymology:** from G73 (ἀγών);

---

## G75

**Greek:** ἀγωνίζομαι

**Transliteration:** *agōnízomai*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to struggle, literally (to compete for a prize), figuratively (to contend with an adversary), or genitive case (to endeavor to accomplish something)

**KJV Equivalents:** fight, labor fervently, strive

**Etymology:** from G73 (ἀγών);

---

## G76

**Greek:** Ἀδάμ

**Transliteration:** *Adám*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Adam, the first man; typically (of Jesus) man (as his representative)

**KJV Equivalents:** Adam

**Etymology:** of Hebrew origin (H0121);

---

## G77

**Greek:** ἀδάπανος

**Transliteration:** *adápanos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  and G1160 (δαπάνη); costless, i.e. gratuitous

**KJV Equivalents:** without expense

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as negative particle);

---

## G78

**Greek:** Ἀδδί

**Transliteration:** *Addí*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  Addi, an Israelite

**KJV Equivalents:** Addi

**Etymology:** probably of Hebrew origin (compare H05716);

---

## G79

**Greek:** ἀδελφή

**Transliteration:** *adelphḗ*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a sister (naturally or ecclesiastically)

**KJV Equivalents:** sister

**Etymology:** feminine of G80 (ἀδελφός);

---

## G80

**Greek:** ἀδελφός

**Transliteration:** *adelphós*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a brother (literally or figuratively) near or remote (much like G1 (Α))

**KJV Equivalents:** brother

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a connective particle) and (the womb);

---

## G81

**Greek:** ἀδελφότης

**Transliteration:** *adelphótēs*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  brotherhood (properly, the feeling of brotherliness), i.e. the (Christian) fraternity

**KJV Equivalents:** brethren, brotherhood

**Etymology:** from G80 (ἀδελφός);

---

## G82

**Greek:** ἄδηλος

**Transliteration:** *ádēlos*

**Part of Speech:** adjective

**Definition:**  hidden, figuratively, indistinct

**KJV Equivalents:** appear not, uncertain

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and G1212 (δῆλος);

---

## G83

**Greek:** ἀδηλότης

**Transliteration:** *adēlótēs*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Definition:**  uncertainty

**KJV Equivalents:** X uncertain

**Etymology:** from G82 (ἄδηλος);

---

## G84

**Greek:** ἀδήλως

**Transliteration:** *adḗlōs*

**Part of Speech:** adverb

**Definition:**  uncertainly

**KJV Equivalents:** uncertainly

**Etymology:** adverb from G82 (ἄδηλος);

---

## G85

**Greek:** ἀδημονέω

**Transliteration:** *adēmonéō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to be in distress (of mind)

**KJV Equivalents:** be full of heaviness, be very heavy

**Etymology:** from a derivative of (to be sated to loathing);

---

## G86

**Greek:** ᾅδης

**Transliteration:** *háidēs*

**Part of Speech:** noun/adjective

**Etymology:** from G1 (Α) (as a negative particle) and a presumed derivative of G2508 (καθαίρω) (meaning cleansed);

**Transliteration:** *anakathízō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  properly, to set up, i.e. (reflexively) to sit up

**KJV Equivalents:** sit up

**Etymology:** from G303 (ἀνά) and G2523 (καθίζω);

---

**Transliteration:** *diaménō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to stay constantly (in being or relation)

**KJV Equivalents:** continue, remain

**Etymology:** from G1223 (διά) and G3306 (μένω);

---

## G1266

**Transliteration:** *diamerízō*

**Etymology:** from G1223 (διά) and G3307 (μερίζω);

**KJV Equivalents:** am, have been, X it is I, was

**Etymology:** the first person singular present indicative; a prolonged form of a primary and defective verb;

**Transliteration:** *eînai*

**KJV Equivalents:** am, was

**Etymology:** present infinitive from G1510 (εἰμί);

## G1722

**Greek:** ἐν

**Transliteration:** *en*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  \

**KJV Equivalents:** about, after, against, + almost, X altogether, among, X as, at, before, between, (here-)by (+ all means), for (… sake of), + give self wholly to, (here-)in(-to, -wardly), X mightily, (because) of, (up-)on, (open-)ly, X outwardly, one, X quickly, X shortly, (speedi-)ly, X that, X there(-in, -on), through(-out), (un-)to(-ward), under, when, where(-with), while, with(-in)

**Etymology:** a primary preposition denoting (fixed) position (in place, time or state), and (by implication) instrumentality (medially or constructively), i.e. a relation of rest (intermediate between G1519 (εἰς) and G1537 (ἐκ));

**Greek:** ἐξίστημι

**Transliteration:** *exístēmi*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to put (stand) out of wits, i.e. astound, or (reflexively) become astounded, insane

**KJV Equivalents:** amaze, be (make) astonished, be beside self (selves), bewitch, wonder

**Etymology:** from G1537 (ἐκ) and G2476 (ἵστημι);

---

## G1909

**Greek:** ἐπί

**Transliteration:** *epí*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  properly, meaning superimposition (of time, place, order, etc.), as a relation of distribution (with the genitive case), i.e. over, upon, etc.; of rest (with the dative case) at, on, etc.; of direction (with the accusative case) towards, upon, etc.

**KJV Equivalents:** about (the times), above, after, against, among, as long as (touching), at, beside, X have charge of, (be-, (where-))fore, in (a place, as much as, the time of, -to), (because) of, (up-)on (behalf of), over, (by, for) the space of, through(-out), (un-)to(-ward), with

**Etymology:** a primary preposition;

---

**KJV Equivalents:** come (into), enter into, go abroad, sit upon, take ship

**KJV Equivalents:** beat into, cast (up-)on, fall, lay (on), put (unto), stretch forth, think on

**Greek:** ἐπιστρέφω

**Transliteration:** *epistréphō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to revert (literally, figuratively or morally)

**KJV Equivalents:** come (go) again, convert, (re-)turn (about, again)

**Etymology:** from G1909 (ἐπί) and G4762 (στρέφω);

---

## G1995

**Greek:** ἐπιστροφή

**Transliteration:** *epistrophḗ*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  reversion, i.e. morally, revolution

**KJV Equivalents:** conversion

**Etymology:** from G1994 (ἐπιστρέφω);

---

## G1996

**Greek:** ἐπισυνάγω

**Transliteration:** *episynágō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to collect upon the same place

**KJV Equivalents:** gather (together)

**Etymology:** from G1909 (ἐπί) and G4863 (συνάγω);

---

## G1997

**Greek:** ἐπισυναγωγή

**Transliteration:** *episynagōgḗ*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a complete collection; especially a Christian meeting (for worship)

**KJV Equivalents:** assembling (gathering) together

**Etymology:** from G1996 (ἐπισυνάγω);

---

## G1998

**Greek:** ἐπισυντρέχω

**Transliteration:** *episyntréchō*

**Part of Speech:** verb

**Definition:**  to hasten together upon one place (or a particular occasion)

**KJV Equivalents:** come running together

**Etymology:** from G1909 (ἐπί) and G4936 (συντρέχω);

---

## G1999

**Greek:** ἐπισύστασις

**Transliteration:** *episýstasis*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  a conspiracy, i.e. concourse (riotous or friendly)

**KJV Equivalents:** that which cometh upon, + raising up

**Etymology:** from the middle voice of a compound of G1909 (ἐπί) and G4921 (συνιστάω);

---

## G2000

**Greek:** ἐπισφαλής

**Transliteration:** *episphalḗs*

**Part of Speech:** unknown

**Definition:**  figuratively, insecure

**KJV Equivalents:** dangerous

**Etymology:** from a compound of G1909 (ἐπί) and (to trip);

---
